[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The stack overflow stems from a mismatch between  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - the _physical_ buffer size in `mg_json_get`:  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m default MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH == [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - and the _logical_ nesting limit in the code’s depth checks:  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m default MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING == [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Since `depth` is allowed to grow up to [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m before bailing out, writing [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` for `depth >= [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m` overruns the [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m-byte stack buffer.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserve Existing Logic**  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must still enforce a maximum nesting level [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msemantic reasons.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter any fuzzing harness, tests, or external dependencies.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing code paths for object [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and array [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m parsing must behave [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentically except for the overflow fix.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Patch Steps**  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In **src/mongoose/src/json.c**, inside `[0m[1;35mmg_json_get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, locate the two blocks[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m` at approximately lines [0m[1;36m166[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m182[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Replace the incorrect guard `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with a guard [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39magainst the actual buffer size. Two equivalent approaches are acceptable:  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Directly use the compile‐time constant:  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Or use `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for future‐proofing:  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Ensure this replacement is applied in both the `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m`–object and `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m`–array cases[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore writing `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;`.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Leave the logical limit `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` untouched; it continues to cap [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msemantic nesting depth, but the _buffer_ cannot exceed `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Example [0m[1;39m([0m[39mObject Case[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```diff[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   + if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m … then:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Rationale**  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Safety**: Bounds the stack write by the actual array size.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Backward compatibility**: No change to public API, path‐matching logic, or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz harness.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Simplicity**: Minimal patch, no new dependencies or utilities.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Side-Effects & Mitigation**  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On deeply nested JSON [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbetween [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m levels[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the parser now errors out [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msooner [0m[1;39m([0m[39mat [0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead of risking memory corruption.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If users explicitly rely on parsing up to [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m levels, they must raise [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand possibly recompile[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to match desired depth.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change does _not_ affect other parts of the codebase or tests, since all [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests expect the prior buffer limit.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **References**  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patched snippet in `test/tls_multirec/patched_mongoose.c` illustrates the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect approach using `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to protect the buffer.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to harness or test code are required; existing test suite and fuzz [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargets will now fail safely rather than corrupt memory.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ASan reports a one-byte write beyond the bounds of the local array `nesting` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `mg_json_get` at line [0m[1;36m186[0m[39m of `json.c`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The invalid write address is exactly at the end of the array’s red-zone, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m in a region allocated for `nesting` spanning bytes [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m61[0m[39m.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The backtrace shows:  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `mg_json_get` → `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` → fuzzer driver code → `main`.  [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/json.[0m[1;92mc:166[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m174[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m166[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'[0m[32m{[0m[32m'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m167[0m[39m:          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m168[0m[39m:          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth == ed && path[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[32m'.'[0m[39m && ci == ei[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m169[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m If we start the object, reset array indices[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m170[0m[39m:            ed++, pos++, ci = ei = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m171[0m[39m:          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m172[0m[39m:          nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m173[0m[39m:          expecting = S_KEY;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m174[0m[39m:          break;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/json.[0m[1;92mc:175[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m182[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m175[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'[0m[32m[[0m[32m'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m176[0m[39m:          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m177[0m[39m:          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth == ed && path[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[32m'[0m[32m[[0m[32m'[0m[39m && ei == ci[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m178[0m[39m:            ed++, pos++, ci = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m179[0m[39m:            for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mei = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; path[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos[0m[1;39m][0m[39m != [0m[32m'[0m[32m][0m[32m'[0m[39m && path[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos[0m[1;39m][0m[39m != [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m; pos++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m180[0m[39m:              ei *= [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m181[0m[39m:              ei += path[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos[0m[1;39m][0m[39m - [0m[32m'0'[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m182[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Core Issue Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The local array `nesting` in `mg_json_get` is declared as `unsigned char [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e. [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m entries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but the code’s depth‐check logic was[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomparing against `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  Thus, depths from [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m up to [0m[1;36m59[0m[39m passed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe check and wrote out-of-bounds, triggering the ASan failure at byte offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The last patch replaced those two checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which *should* have prevented any write at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdepth ≥[0m[1;36m30[0m[39m.  Yet the fuzzer still overflows `nesting` at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e. [0m[33mdepth[0m[39m==[0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating one of the following:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m *Not all* code paths that write into `nesting` are guarded by the new [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m The patch mistakenly used the wrong macro in one of the branches, or the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode path at line [0m[1;36m186[0m[39m was not covered by the two patched sites.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A review of the full `mg_json_get` function shows **two** distinct [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` writes:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • One immediately after the `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` check [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround original line [0m[1;36m172[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A second one after the `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m` parsing logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround original line [0m[1;36m186[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The last patch only altered the checks at the opening‐brace site and the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*entry* into the `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m` branch, but did *not* update the depth guard *just before* the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecond `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` statement.  That explains why the fuzzer still drives [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`depth` up to [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m and overflows.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Fix[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. **Identify and Protect All Writes to `nesting`**  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      i.  Locate *every* statement of the form `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = …;` in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_json_get`.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ii. Ensure immediately before each such write, there is a guard:  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          This protects against writing at `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` or beyond.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. **Use a Single Constant**  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` entirely in this function with [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`, since that is the actual buffer size.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Optionally, for even stronger self-documentation, one could use a [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompile‐time assertion or `[0m[1;35mstatic_assert[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mkeep them in sync.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. **Maintain Existing Logic**  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Do not change the harness, error codes, or array indexing logic beyond [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madding the necessary check.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - All existing code paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue parsing, key parsing, colon/comma [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanagement[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain unchanged except for inserting or correcting the boundary check.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. **Review Adjacent Path‐Parsing Code**  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - While the overflow sits in `nesting`, review that the `ci`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`ei` parsing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloop does not write beyond any buffers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mit operates on `path`, which is supplied by[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe caller[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  No code modifications are needed here unless future overflows appear [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `path`.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Step-by-Step Implementation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `src/mongoose/src/json.c`.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Search for all occurrences of `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Immediately above *each* occurrence, insert or replace the guard with:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Remove any remaining references to `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` in `mg_json_get` so [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat there is a single source of truth [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Rebuild and rerun the libFuzzer harness for >[0m[1;36m1000[0m[39m iterations to confirm no [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfurther ASan stack‐buffer‐overflow in `nesting`.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Correctness**: By aligning the depth guard to the actual buffer size, we [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminate the off‐by‐one that allowed writes beyond `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m29[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Minimal Impact**: We do not alter any parsing logic except for adding [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary checks, so existing functionality [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding error codes and return [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Safety**: The check is placed immediately before every potential write site,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring no slip through.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Maintainability**: Consolidating on `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` prevents macro [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmismatches in the future. A `static_assert` could be added to guarantee [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer/macro consistency at compile time.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Performance**: A single integer comparison before a push is negligible [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverhead in JSON parsing.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - *Slightly increased code size* [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtwo extra `if` statements[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m — negligible for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39membedded contexts.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If someone expected deeper nesting [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, this patch reduces maximum [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdepth to [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m.  However, since `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` was only sized for [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m to begin with, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msupporting deeper nesting would have required reallocating a larger buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout‐of‐scope[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other buffers or external logic are affected.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Previous issue logs and ASan backtraces consistently report writes to [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`nesting` at offsets ≥[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The header defines `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` as [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m, matching the buffer declaration.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar patterns in other code [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. `path` parsing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m always guard against [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer size before writes; we emulate that pattern here.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtesting with AddressSanitizer reporting a stack-buffer-overflow in the local [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow occurs when writing `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;`. The runtime value of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`depth` at overflow reaches the length of the `nesting` array, causing a write just[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpast its end.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2782[0m[39m:          break;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root‐Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack‐buffer‐overflow is caused by a mismatch between the size of the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`nesting` array and the depth checks guarding writes into it.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - In both `src/json.c` and the monolithic `mongoose.c`, the parser allocates  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         `unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       but checks against `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor a mixture of [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, allowing `depth` to reach values ≥ [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` before guarding, then writing `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` out-of-bounds.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The initial patch tightened some comparisons in `src/json.c` to use [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`, but:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m It did not apply to the monolithic build [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mongoose.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which still uses [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m The fix in `src/json.c` was asymmetrical [0m[1;39m([0m[39monly partial branches were fully [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguarded[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and mixed `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must ensure the buffer capacity and its guard threshold match exactly, in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mevery code path, and in all build variants.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Overall Strategy[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Unify on one macro [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for both buffer sizing and overflow [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Keep the existing buffer declaration of `unsigned char [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace *all* comparisons of `depth` against `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` with [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomparisons against `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Use `>= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` to guard *before* every `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Apply the same patches to both `src/json.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe standalone parser[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mongoose.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe monolithic one[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, in each branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Remove stray or redundant `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` checks, and ensure exactly [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone `>= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` guard immediately before each depth increment.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In `src/json.c`:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Locate the `nesting` buffer at the top of `mg_json_get`:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```c[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        *Leave this unchanged.*[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For the `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` branch:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Change any `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```c[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Remove any other stale checks of `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Ensure this single check precedes the line:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```c[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'[0m[32m{[0m[32m'[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For the `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m` branch:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Similarly replace the initial `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```c[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Eliminate any extra or duplicated `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` tests.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Confirm this guard is immediately before:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```c[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'[0m[32m[[0m[32m'[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In `mongoose.c`:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Locate the monolithic copy of `mg_json_get` around lines [0m[1;36m2726[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m2733[0m[39m:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```c[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        *Leave the buffer sizing macro as is.*[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In the `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m2763[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m2769[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Replace `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```c[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Remove any other references to `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` in that block.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In the `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m` branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m2772[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m2782[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Similarly replace the initial `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```c[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ```[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Eliminate any extra `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` checks, making sure one `>= [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` guard directly precedes `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'[0m[32m[[0m[32m'[0m[39m;`.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do **not** alter the fuzz‐harness, nor any JSON‐path logic—only the depth [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks that prevent buffer overflows.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By using the same macro [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for both buffer and checks, no [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnew code paths are introduced or removed.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The JSON‐too‐deep error will now trigger at the correct threshold [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`depth == [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in *all* build variants.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The maximum allowed nesting is now strictly `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefault [0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregardless of `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`.  Users who previously set [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` > `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` will see earlier failures—but this [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mearlier limit matches the actual buffer size.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If consumers truly need deeper nesting [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, they should raise [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` accordingly at compile time.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This strategy keeps the public API and test suite intact, only tightening the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdepth guard to eliminate the overflow.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Testing[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild both the standalone and monolithic parsers.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rerun the libFuzzer target with the previously failing testcase.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm the ASan‐detected stack‐buffer‐overflow no longer occurs, and a clean [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“too deep” error is returned instead.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
